I would compare phones to cars.  Some buy iphones for luxury , like cars. It's like buying a super car because it is about luxury . However there are some , who like me , care more about performance. There's lots of cars that are expensive but some Tuners and Muscle cars are cheaper and yet fast. If I wanna drive 300KM/h , I want to choose a safe and budget supercar ( basically still expensive but it's like slightly less expensive ) . Same with Iphones altho if one is not into iphones they can buy gaming phones like red magic 10 pro + . Gaming phones are actually good for everything but gaming ( Because you don't want to play mobile games , atleast that's my opinion ). So even if you do or not , gaming phones have a lot of headroom to use for powerful task and emulation.

It's the same feel sometimes I feel when people buy iphones but not use it to fullest or celebraties buying super cars but keeping them stored. Most super cars don't even go 150Km/h. And I know it's not my business but since topic is this I said. Ofc when I said 300Km/h I meant race tracks , legal and safe.
I always wanted to buy R34 Nissan for speed , I thought it's like a budget flagship phone kind of car version. Honestly if it reaches even 280Km/h is fine. Speed is also not always fun , so I get people buying best of best. Even for iphone's defense is it actually is important for some to buy a flagship. Some people don't have PC , and maybe not even laptop or if then also a Powerful phone is very helpful at certain times.
If you buy cheap phones , it's not good when you are in need. Powerful phone means you can do many things a pc can do anywhere , despite doing it in a limited screen and lack of keyboard. If I type this comment in phone I would have passed away from auto correct and patience. I get it but ,I think one way to look at powerful phones is they can come in handy. I use gaming laptop for my work. Sure it's like using a fast car for basic groceries , but it also means I can use power tasks anytime I want without having to get another pc . Same with that car , who can speed up at emergencies.

As someone who has a A10 for main phone  ( 2/32  + Exynos 7884B ) and even a Redmi 14c recently ( I love collecting if I can afford ) , the A10 is fine for most task but due to lags Redmi 14c is better , despte of 720p LCD it's not easy to pixel peep from a bit distance , and from this I can say what you mean is right. Not everyone needs a powerful phone. But if I play games it lags hard. That's where my One plus comes .
Same with my pc vs laptop , both are same specs for basic tasks . One doesn't have a gpu (pc )  
I made sure my pc boots almost as fast if not faster than my laptop. So basically I can boot my pc or laptop and it still turns on same , leaving my pc for home tasks and office tasks on laptop. But if I want to do power task it's possible only on laptop. but this is my lifestyle and it won't suit everyone.

So It's either them to get a midrange phones , or even flagship ( older ) Android or This iphone. 
I recommend this iphone just for 120hz. You don't need it maybe , but at this price point you deserve it ( atleast if you like apple )
For me I always lean to gaming phones or some chinese phones to collect. Even I don't play much games on android , but it is important to have a mid range chip just in case.
Personally as a Spec lover , I can't deny I'm on the other spectrum of this
